##  Repository Structure

```sh
└── FFCKbot.git/
    ├── README.md
    ├── README.md~
    ├── commands
    │   └── course.js
    ├── config.json
    ├── deploy-commands.js
    ├── fonctions
    │   ├── Infocourse.js
    │   ├── chanels.js
    │   └── createCourse.js
    ├── index.js
    ├── node_modules
    │   ├── .package-lock.json
    │   ├── @discordjs
    │   ├── @sapphire
    │   ├── @types
    │   ├── @vladfrangu
    │   ├── busboy
    │   ├── discord-api-types
    │   ├── discord.js
    │   ├── fast-deep-equal
    │   ├── lodash
    │   ├── lodash.snakecase
    │   ├── magic-bytes.js
    │   ├── node.js
    │   ├── nodejs
    │   ├── streamsearch
    │   ├── ts-mixer
    │   ├── tslib
    │   ├── undici
    │   └── ws
    ├── package-lock.json
    └── package.json
```

##  Getting Started

###  Prerequisites

**JavaScript**: `version x.y.z`

###  Installation

Build the project from source:

1. Clone the FFCKbot.git repository:
```sh
❯ git clone https://github.com/TitouanGIT/FFCKbot.git
```

2. Navigate to the project directory:
```sh
❯ cd FFCKbot.git
```

3. Install the required dependencies:
```sh
❯ npm install
```

###  Usage

To run the project, execute the following command:

```sh
❯ node app.js
```

###  Tests

Execute the test suite using the following command:

```sh
❯ npm test
```

##  Contributing

Contributions are welcome! Here are several ways you can contribute:

- **[Report Issues](https://github.com/TitouanGIT/FFCKbot.git/issues)**: Submit bugs found or log feature requests for the `FFCKbot.git` project.
- **[Submit Pull Requests](https://github.com/TitouanGIT/FFCKbot.git/blob/main/CONTRIBUTING.md)**: Review open PRs, and submit your own PRs.
- **[Join the Discussions](https://github.com/TitouanGIT/FFCKbot.git/discussions)**: Share your insights, provide feedback, or ask questions.

<details closed>
<summary>Contributing Guidelines</summary>

1. **Fork the Repository**: Start by forking the project repository to your github account.
2. **Clone Locally**: Clone the forked repository to your local machine using a git client.
   ```sh
   git clone https://github.com/TitouanGIT/FFCKbot.git
   ```
3. **Create a New Branch**: Always work on a new branch, giving it a descriptive name.
   ```sh
   git checkout -b new-feature-x
   ```
4. **Make Your Changes**: Develop and test your changes locally.
5. **Commit Your Changes**: Commit with a clear message describing your updates.
   ```sh
   git commit -m 'Implemented new feature x.'
   ```
6. **Push to github**: Push the changes to your forked repository.
   ```sh
   git push origin new-feature-x
   ```
7. **Submit a Pull Request**: Create a PR against the original project repository. Clearly describe the changes and their motivations.
8. **Review**: Once your PR is reviewed and approved, it will be merged into the main branch. Congratulations on your contribution!
</details>

<details closed>
<summary>Contributor Graph</summary>
<br>
<p align="left">
   <a href="https://github.com{/TitouanGIT/FFCKbot.git/}graphs/contributors">
      <img src="https://contrib.rocks/image?repo=TitouanGIT/FFCKbot.git">
   </a>
</p>
</details>
